## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> idle
  idle --> fetching : fetchDomainData called
  fetching --> success : axios.get resolves
  fetching --> error : axios.get rejects
  success --> dispatching : dispatch RECEIVE_HEALTHCARE_DOMAIN_DATA
  dispatching --> updatingState : reducer processes action
  updatingState --> idle : state updated (assets assigned)
  error --> idle : exception thrown
```
